  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2  1 fellowship program to provide funds to nursing schools in the
  2  2 state, including but not limited to nursing schools located at
  2  3 community colleges, for fellowships for individuals employed in
  2  4 qualifying positions on the nursing faculty. The program shall
  2  5 be designed to assist nursing schools in filling vacancies in
  2  6 qualifying positions throughout the state.
  2  7    b.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2  8 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2  9 association, and in cooperation with nursing schools throughout
  2 10 the state, shall develop a distribution formula which shall
  2 11 provide that no more than thirty percent of the available
  2 12 moneys are awarded to a single nursing school. Additionally,
  2 13 the program shall limit funding for a qualifying position in a
  2 14 nursing school to no more than ten thousand dollars per year
  2 15 for up to three years.
  2 16    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2 17 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2 18 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A to
  2 19 administer the program. The rules shall include provisions
  2 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying position at a nursing
  2 21 school.
  2 22    d.  In determining eligibility for a fellowship, the
  2 23 department shall consider all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  The length of time a qualifying position has gone
  2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.

  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2  5 be designed to assist nursing schools in filling vacancies in
  2  6 qualifying positions throughout the state.
  2  7    b.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2  8 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2  9 association, and in cooperation with nursing schools throughout
  2 10 the state, shall develop a distribution formula which shall
  2 11 provide that no more than thirty percent of the available
  2 12 moneys are awarded to a single nursing school. Additionally,
  2 13 the program shall limit funding for a qualifying position in a
  2 14 nursing school to no more than ten thousand dollars per year
  2 15 for up to three years.
  2 16    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2 17 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2 18 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A to
  2 19 administer the program. The rules shall include provisions
  2 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying position at a nursing
  2 21 school.
  2 22    d.  In determining eligibility for a fellowship, the
  2 23 department shall consider all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  The length of time a qualifying position has gone
  2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.
  3 22    4.  Nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  3 23 program.
  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.

  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2 10 the state, shall develop a distribution formula which shall
  2 11 provide that no more than thirty percent of the available
  2 12 moneys are awarded to a single nursing school. Additionally,
  2 13 the program shall limit funding for a qualifying position in a
  2 14 nursing school to no more than ten thousand dollars per year
  2 15 for up to three years.
  2 16    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2 17 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2 18 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A to
  2 19 administer the program. The rules shall include provisions
  2 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying position at a nursing
  2 21 school.
  2 22    d.  In determining eligibility for a fellowship, the
  2 23 department shall consider all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  The length of time a qualifying position has gone
  2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.

  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2 15 for up to three years.
  2 16    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  2 17 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  2 18 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A to
  2 19 administer the program. The rules shall include provisions
  2 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying position at a nursing
  2 21 school.
  2 22    d.  In determining eligibility for a fellowship, the
  2 23 department shall consider all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  The length of time a qualifying position has gone
  2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.

  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying position at a nursing
  2 21 school.
  2 22    d.  In determining eligibility for a fellowship, the
  2 23 department shall consider all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  The length of time a qualifying position has gone
  2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.

  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   2 25 unfilled at a nursing school.
  2 26    (2)  Documented recruiting efforts by a nursing school.
  2 27    (3)  The geographic location of a nursing school.
  2 28    (4)  The type of nursing program offered at the nursing
  2 29 school, including associate, bachelor's, master's, or doctoral
  2 30 degrees in nursing, and the need for the specific nursing
  2 31 program in the state.
  2 32    3.  Nurse educator scholarship program.
  2 33    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.
  3 22    4.  Nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  3 23 program.
  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.

  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:

  2 34 scholarship program. The goal of the nurse educator
  2 35 scholarship program is to address the waiting list of qualified
  3  1 applicants to Iowa's nursing schools by providing incentives
  3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing

  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private

  3  9 the state board of regents.

  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount

  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.

  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions

  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.
  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   3  2 for the training of additional nursing educators. For the
  3  3 purposes of this subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered
  3  4 nurse who holds a master's degree or doctorate degree and is
  3  5 employed as a faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing
  3  6 education program as provided in rules adopted by the board
  3  7 of nursing at a community college, an accredited private
  3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.

  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   3  8 institution, or an institution of higher education governed by
  3  9 the state board of regents.
  3 10    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  3 11 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  3 12 program shall provide for scholarship payments in an amount
  3 13 established by rule for students who are preparing to teach in
  3 14 qualifying teaching positions.
  3 15    c.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  3 16 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  3 17 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A relating
  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.
  3 22    4.  Nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  3 23 program.
  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.

  3 18 to the establishment and administration of the nurse educator
  3 19 scholarship program. The rules shall include provisions
  3 20 specifying what constitutes a qualifying teaching position and
  3 21 the amount of any scholarship.
  3 22    4.  Nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  3 23 program.
  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
  4 31    5.  Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund established. An
  4 32 Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund is created in the state
  4 33 treasury as a separate fund under the control of the department
  4 34 for deposit of moneys appropriated to or received by the
  4 35 department for use under the initiative. Notwithstanding
  5  1 section 8.33, moneys deposited in the fund shall not revert
  5  2 to any fund of the state at the end of any fiscal year but
  5  3 shall remain in the Iowa needs nurses now initiative fund and
  5  4 be continuously available for the purposes of the initiative.
  5  5 Notwithstanding section 12C.7, subsection 2, interest or
  5  6 earnings on moneys deposited in the fund shall be credited to
  5  7 the fund.

  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   3 23 program.
  3 24    a.  The department shall establish a nurse educator
  3 25 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program. The goal of the
  3 26 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program is
  3 27 to address the waiting list of qualified applicants to Iowa's
  3 28 nursing schools by providing incentives for the education
  3 29 of additional nursing educators. For the purposes of this
  3 30 subsection, "nurse educator" means a registered nurse who holds
  3 31 a master's degree or doctorate degree and is employed as a
  3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing
  3 34 at a community college, an accredited private institution, or
  3 35 an institution of higher education governed by the state board
  4  1 of regents.
  4  2    b.  The program shall consist of scholarships to further
  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.

  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   3 32 faculty member who teaches nursing in a nursing education
  3 33 program as provided in rules adopted by the board of nursing

  4  1 of regents.

  4  3 advance the education of nurses to become nurse educators. The
  4  4 program shall provide for scholarship=in=exchange=for=service
  4  5 payments in an amount established by rule for students who
  4  6 are preparing to teach in qualifying teaching positions for a
  4  7 period of not less than four consecutive academic years.
  4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.

  5  8    Sec. 2.  Section 261.2, subsection 8, Code 2017, is amended
  5  9 to read as follows:
  5 10    8.  Submit by January 15 annually a report to the general
  5 11 assembly which provides, by program, the number of individuals
  5 12 who received loan forgiveness   4  8    c.  The scholarship=in=exchange=for=service recipient
  4  9 and the department shall enter into an agreement specifying
  4 10 the obligations of the applicant and the department.
  4 11 If the nurse educator leaves the qualifying teaching
  4 12 position prior to teaching for four consecutive academic
  4 13 years, the nurse educator shall be liable to repay the
  4 14 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service amount to the state plus
  4 15 interest as specified by rule. However, if the nurse educator
  4 16 leaves the qualified teaching position involuntarily, the nurse
  4 17 educator shall be liable to repay only a pro rata amount of the
  4 18 scholarship based on incomplete years of service.
  4 19    d.  The receipt of a nurse educator
  4 20 scholarship=in=exchange=for=service shall not impact
  4 21 eligibility of an individual for other financial incentives
  4 22 including but not limited to loan forgiveness programs.
  4 23    e.  The department, in consultation with the board of
  4 24 nursing, the department of education, and the Iowa nurses
  4 25 association, shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter 17A
  4 26 relating to the establishment and administration of the
  4 27 nurse educator scholarship=in=exchange=for=service program.
  4 28 The rules shall include the provisions specifying what
  4 29 constitutes a qualifying teaching position and the amount of
  4 30 any scholarship=in=exchange=for=service.
